## 🔍 Cross-Page Patterns: Common HTML Issues

These HTML patterns cause the same accessibility errors across multiple pages. **Fix the pattern once in your codebase to fix it everywhere!**

### 🎯 Top Patterns to Fix (Highest Impact)

#### Pattern 1: Affects 43 page(s) - 274 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: ALFA
**Rule**: [SIA-R43: No description](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r43)
**Issue**: The `<svg>` element does not have an accessible name

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<svg viewBox="0 0 13 12" class="bpa-icon bpa-icon-link-external" width="13" height="12" version="1.1" role="img" focusable="false">...</svg>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
/svg[@class="bpa-icon bpa-icon-link-external"]
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('/svg[@class="bpa-icon bpa-icon-link-external"]')`
5. The element will be highlighted

**Affected Pages**:
- https://bundesregierung.de/breg-de
- https://bundesregierung.de/breg-de/barrierefreiheit?view=
- https://bundesregierung.de/breg-de/barrierefreiheit/barrierefreiheit-feedback?view=
- https://bundesregierung.de/breg-de/service/kontakt
- https://bundesregierung.de/breg-de/service/kontakt/kontaktformular?view=
- *...and 38 more page(s)*

#### Pattern 2: Affects 43 page(s) - 268 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: ALFA
**Rule**: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)
**Issue**: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<p>...</p>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):

```
/p
```

#### Pattern 3: Affects 43 page(s) - 268 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: axe
**Rule**: [svg-img-alt](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/svg-img-alt?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious
**Issue**: <svg> elements with an img role must have alternative text

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<svg viewBox="0 0 13 12" class="bpa-icon bpa-icon-link-external" width="13" height="12" version="1.1" role="img" focusable="false">
<use href="#icon-link-external"></use>
</svg>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
.bpa-link-internal > .bpa-icon-link-external[width="13"][viewBox="0 0 13 12"]
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('.bpa-link-internal > .bpa-icon-link-external[width="13"][viewBox="0 0 13 12"]')`
5. The element will be highlighted

**Affected Pages**:
- https://bundesregierung.de/breg-de
- https://bundesregierung.de/breg-de/barrierefreiheit?view=
- https://bundesregierung.de/breg-de/barrierefreiheit/barrierefreiheit-feedback?view=
- https://bundesregierung.de/breg-de/service/kontakt
- https://bundesregierung.de/breg-de/service/kontakt/kontaktformular?view=
- *...and 38 more page(s)*

#### Pattern 5: Affects 43 page(s) - 115 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: axe
**Rule**: [svg-img-alt](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/svg-img-alt?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious
**Issue**: <svg> elements with an img role must have alternative text

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<svg viewBox="0 0 14 14" class="bpa-icon bpa-icon-close" width="14" height="14" version="1.1" role="img" focusable="false">
<use href="#icon-close"></use>
</svg>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
.bpa-icon-wrapper:nth-child(3) > .bpa-icon-close[width="14"][viewBox="0 0 14 14"]
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('.bpa-icon-wrapper:nth-child(3) > .bpa-icon-close[width="14"][viewBox="0 0 14 14"]')`

```html
<a href="https://www.youtube.com/bundesregierung" target="_blank" title="Externer Link: Zum YouTube-Kanal der Bundesregierung (Öffnet neues Fenster)" class="bpa-link-icon" rel="noopener noreferrer">...</a>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
/a[@class="bpa-link-icon"]
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('/a[@class="bpa-link-icon"]')`
5. The element will be highlighted

**Affected Pages**:
- https://bundesregierung.de/breg-de
- https://bundesregierung.de/breg-de/barrierefreiheit?view=
- https://bundesregierung.de/breg-de/barrierefreiheit/barrierefreiheit-feedback?view=
- https://bundesregierung.de/breg-de/service/kontakt
- https://bundesregierung.de/breg-de/service/kontakt/kontaktformular?view=
- *...and 38 more page(s)*

---

> 💡 **Pro Tip**: These patterns likely come from shared components or templates in your codebase. Fix them in the component/template source, and the fix will propagate to all affected pages.

## Detailed Failure Information (ALFA)

### https://bundesregierung.de/breg-de

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button class="bpa-toggledown-title" data-toggledown="toggledown-content-5-2b2yo3bftyilwvwl23txcxutt" aria-expanded="false">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="bpa-toggledown-title"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="https://www.bundesregierung.de/breg-en" target="_self" aria-label="Open page in English" class="bpa-link-small" lang="en"> English </a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="bpa-link-small"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="#" target="_self" class="bpa-link-small bpa-link-icon bpa-meta-menu-button" role="button" aria-expanded="false" aria-haspopup="dialog" aria-controls="bpa-nav-meta-flyout">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="bpa-link-small bpa-link-icon bpa-meta-menu-button"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="https://www.bundesregierung.de/breg-de/schwerpunkte/das-kann-deutschland" target="_self" class="bpa-link-flyout-focus"> Das kann Deutschland </a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="bpa-link-flyout-focus"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="https://www.bundesregierung.de/breg-de/schwerpunkte" target="_self" class="bpa-link-flyout-default"> Schwerpunkte  </a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="bpa-link-flyout-default"]`

*... and 11 more failures for this rule*

#### Rule: [SIA-R18: ARIA states are consistent with element semantics](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r18)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The attribute is not allowed for the element on which it is specified

#### Rule: [SIA-R3: lang attribute has a valid language code](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r3)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<div id="bpa-searchapp-react-json" data-json-base-url="https://www.bundesregierung.de/breg-de/suche/992800!searchJson" />`
- XPath: `/div[@id="bpa-searchapp-react-json"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<div id="bpa-search-inner" class="bpa-search-inner">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="bpa-search-inner"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<form id="bpa-searchapp-form">...</form>`
- XPath: `/form[@id="bpa-searchapp-form"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R43](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r43)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The `<svg>` element does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<svg viewBox="0 0 13 12" class="bpa-icon bpa-icon-link-external" width="13" height="12" version="1.1" role="img" focusable="false">...</svg>`
- XPath: `/svg[@class="bpa-icon bpa-icon-link-external"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The `<svg>` element does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<svg viewBox="0 0 14 14" class="bpa-icon bpa-icon-close" width="14" height="14" version="1.1" role="img" focusable="false">...</svg>`
- XPath: `/svg[@class="bpa-icon bpa-icon-close"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The `<svg>` element does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<svg viewBox="0 0 19 16" class="bpa-icon bpa-icon-playlist" width="19" height="16" version="1.1" role="img" focusable="false">...</svg>`
- XPath: `/svg[@class="bpa-icon bpa-icon-playlist"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The `<svg>` element does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="bpa-icon bpa-icon-plus" width="16" height="16" version="1.1" role="img" focusable="false">...</svg>`
- XPath: `/svg[@class="bpa-icon bpa-icon-plus"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The `<svg>` element does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<svg viewBox="0 0 16 14" class="bpa-icon bpa-icon-arrow-left" width="16" height="14" version="1.1" role="img" focusable="false">...</svg>`
- XPath: `/svg[@class="bpa-icon bpa-icon-arrow-left"]`

*... and 5 more failures for this rule*

#### Rule: [SIA-R54](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r54)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The assertive region is not atomic
- HTML: `<section class="bpa-toast" aria-live="assertive">...</section>`
- XPath: `/section[@class="bpa-toast"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R56: Landmarks with the same role are distinguishable](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r56)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Some `navigation` have the same name.

#### Rule: [SIA-R57: Landmarks don't repeat the same content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r57)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text is not included in a landmark region

#### Rule: [SIA-R66: Text has enhanced contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r66)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 5.3:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p>...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="bpa-short-text">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="bpa-short-text"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="bpa-topline-title-wrapper ">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="bpa-topline-title-wrapper "]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R87: First focusable element is a skip link](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r87)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The first tabbable element in the document is not a semantic link

- Message: The `<svg>` element does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<svg viewBox="0 0 14 14" class="bpa-icon bpa-icon-close" width="14" height="14" version="1.1" role="img" focusable="false">...</svg>`

**Failure 3:**

- HTML: `<svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="bpa-icon bpa-icon-plus" width="16" height="16" version="1.1" role="img" focusable="false">...</svg>`
- XPath: `/svg[@class="bpa-icon bpa-icon-plus"]`

**Failure 4:**

- XPath: `/svg[@class="bpa-icon bpa-icon-close"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The `<svg>` element does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="bpa-icon bpa-icon-plus" width="16" height="16" version="1.1" role="img" focusable="false">...</svg>`
- XPath: `/svg[@class="bpa-icon bpa-icon-plus"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The `<svg>` element does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<svg viewBox="0 0 22 22" class="bpa-icon bpa-icon-time" width="22" height="22" version="1.1" role="img" aria-labelledby="aria-97-34j2yyvel2g1vhigeuhwibeen" focusable="false">...</svg>`
- XPath: `/svg[@class="bpa-icon bpa-icon-time"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The `<svg>` element does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<svg viewBox="0 0 13 16" class="bpa-icon bpa-icon-player-play" width="13" height="16" version="1.1" role="img" focusable="false">...</svg>`
- XPath: `/svg[@class="bpa-icon bpa-icon-player-play"]`

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 5.54:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p>...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="bpa-short-text">Stefan Kornelius ist sowohl Sprecher der Bundesreg...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="bpa-short-text"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="bpa-article-header-reading-time">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="bpa-article-header-reading-time"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p class="bpa-topline-title-wrapper ">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="bpa-topline-title-wrapper "]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R78: Headings of same level have text content between them](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r78)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: There is no content between this heading and the next
- HTML: `<h3 class="bpa-topline-title-wrapper ">...</h3>`
- XPath: `/h3[@class="bpa-topline-title-wrapper "]`

## Detailed Failure Information (axe)

### https://bundesregierung.de/breg-de

#### Rule: [aria-allowed-attr](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-allowed-attr?application=playwright)
**Impact**: critical

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Elements must only use supported ARIA attributes
- HTML: `<input class="form-control" id="cookie-allow-necessary" type="checkbox" value="cookie-allow-necessary" name="cookie-allow-necessary" aria-selected="true" disabled="" checked="">`
- XPath: `#cookie-allow-necessary`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Elements must only use supported ARIA attributes
- HTML: `<input class="form-control" id="cookie-allow-tracking" type="checkbox" value="cookie-allow-tracking" name="cookie-allow-tracking" aria-selected="false">`
- XPath: `#cookie-allow-tracking`

#### Rule: [aria-required-children](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-required-children?application=playwright)
**Impact**: critical

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Certain ARIA roles must contain particular children
- HTML: `<div class="swiper swiper-virtual swiper-initialized swiper-horizontal swiper-watch-progress" role="list">`
- XPath: `#stage-widget,.css-1orjcoo > .swiper.swiper-virtual.swiper-initialized`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Certain ARIA roles must contain particular children
- HTML: `<div class="swiper swiper-virtual swiper-initialized swiper-horizontal swiper-watch-progress" role="list" style="height: 100%; width: 100%;">`
- XPath: `#stage-widget,.swiper-slide-active.swiper-slide-visible[data-swiper-slide-index="0"] > .css-ncluv0 > .css-1bq2o3o > .css-1rbl84u[role="region"][aria-roledescription="carousel"] > .swiper.swiper-virtual.swiper-initialized`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Certain ARIA roles must contain particular children
- HTML: `<div class="swiper swiper-virtual swiper-initialized swiper-horizontal swiper-watch-progress" role="list" style="height: 100%; width: 100%;">`
- XPath: `#stage-widget,.swiper-slide-next.swiper-slide-visible[data-swiper-slide-index="1"] > .css-ncluv0 > .css-1bq2o3o > .css-1rbl84u[role="region"][aria-roledescription="carousel"] > .swiper.swiper-virtual.swiper-initialized`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Certain ARIA roles must contain particular children
- HTML: `<div class="swiper swiper-virtual swiper-initialized swiper-horizontal swiper-watch-progress" role="list" style="height: 100%; width: 100%;">`
- XPath: `#stage-widget,.swiper-slide-visible.swiper-slide-fully-visible[data-swiper-slide-index="2"] > .css-ncluv0 > .css-1bq2o3o > .css-1rbl84u[role="region"][aria-roledescription="carousel"] > .swiper.swiper-virtual.swiper-initialized`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Certain ARIA roles must contain particular children
- HTML: `<div class="swiper swiper-virtual swiper-initialized swiper-horizontal swiper-watch-progress" role="list" style="height: 100%; width: 100%;">`
- XPath: `#stage-widget,div[data-swiper-slide-index="3"] > .css-ncluv0 > .css-1bq2o3o > .css-1rbl84u[role="region"][aria-roledescription="carousel"] > .swiper.swiper-virtual.swiper-initialized`

*... and 2 more failures for this rule*

#### Rule: [landmark-unique](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/landmark-unique?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Landmarks should have a unique role or role/label/title (i.e. accessible name) combination
- HTML: `<nav class="bpa-menu-search" aria-labelledby="main-menu-flyout-title">`
- XPath: `nav[aria-labelledby="main-menu-flyout-title"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Landmarks should have a unique role or role/label/title (i.e. accessible name) combination
- HTML: `<div role="region" aria-roledescription="carousel" class="css-1orjcoo">`
- XPath: `#stage-widget,.css-1orjcoo`

#### Rule: [region](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/region?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: All page content should be contained by landmarks
- HTML: `<h1 class="bpa-accessibility">Bundesregierung \| Startseite</h1>`
- XPath: `.bpa-accessibility`

#### Rule: [svg-img-alt](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/svg-img-alt?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious

**Failure 1:**
- Message: <svg> elements with an img role must have alternative text
- HTML: `<svg viewBox="0 0 13 12" class="bpa-icon bpa-icon-link-external" width="13" height="12" version="1.1" role="img" focusable="false"> <use href="#icon-link-external"></use> </svg>`
- XPath: `.bpa-link-internal > .bpa-icon-link-external[width="13"][viewBox="0 0 13 12"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: <svg> elements with an img role must have alternative text
- HTML: `<svg viewBox="0 0 14 14" class="bpa-icon bpa-icon-close" width="14" height="14" version="1.1" role="img" focusable="false"> <use href="#icon-close"></use> </svg>`
- XPath: `.bpa-icon-wrapper:nth-child(3) > .bpa-icon-close[width="14"][viewBox="0 0 14 14"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: <svg> elements with an img role must have alternative text
- HTML: `<svg viewBox="0 0 14 14" class="bpa-icon bpa-icon-close" width="14" height="14" version="1.1" role="img" focusable="false"> <use href="#icon-close"></use> </svg>`
- XPath: `.bpa-hero-teaser-share > .bpa-share.bpa-popover-wrapper.bpa-right > .bpa-share-list > .bpa-share-links-item:nth-child(3) > .bpa-popover-button.js-btn-share.bpa-share-btn > .bpa-btn-icon-before > .bpa-icon-close[width="14"][viewBox="0 0 14 14"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: <svg> elements with an img role must have alternative text
- HTML: `<svg viewBox="0 0 19 16" class="bpa-icon bpa-icon-playlist" width="19" height="16" version="1.1" role="img" focusable="false"> <use href="#icon-playlist"></use> </svg>`
- XPath: `.bpa-icon-playlist`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: <svg> elements with an img role must have alternative text
- HTML: `<svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="bpa-icon bpa-icon-plus" width="16" height="16" version="1.1" role="img" focusable="false"> <use href="#icon-plus"></use> </svg>`
- XPath: `.js-show-more > .bpa-icon-wrapper > .bpa-icon-plus[height="16"][width="16"]`

*... and 9 more failures for this rule*

### https://bundesregierung.de/breg-de/barrierefreiheit?view=

#### Rule: [aria-allowed-attr](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-allowed-attr?application=playwright)

**Failure 1:**

- HTML: `<input class="form-control" id="cookie-allow-necessary" type="checkbox" value="cookie-allow-necessary" name="cookie-allow-necessary" aria-selected="true" disabled="" checked="">`
- XPath: `#cookie-allow-necessary`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Elements must only use supported ARIA attributes

- HTML: `<h3 class="bpa-topline-title-wrapper "> <span class="bpa-topline"> <span class="bpa-topline-title"> Bundesregierung </span> </span> <span class="bpa-teaser-title"> <span class="bpa-teaser-title-text"> <span class="bpa-teaser-title-text-inner"> Bundeskanzleramt </span> </span> </span> </h3>`
- XPath: `.bpa-teaser-wrapper:nth-child(1) > .bpa-teaser > .bpa-teaser-main-content.js-teaser-module-with-link.js-linked > .bpa-teaser-inner-image > .bpa-teaser-text-wrapper > .bpa-link[target="_self"] > .bpa-topline-title-wrapper`

#### Rule: [landmark-unique](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/landmark-unique?application=playwright)
